   function launchAssistant() {

	// open a blank "target" window
	// or get the reference to the existing "target" window
	var upassistWin = window.open('', 'macupassistant', 'scrollbars=1,resizable=0,location=0,height=500,width=500,top=300,left=300', true);
	console.log('mac assistant window open called, no URL');

	// if the "target" window was just opened, change its url
	if(upassistWin.location.href === 'about:blank') {
		upassistWin.location.href = 'https://eshop.macsales.com/api/upgrade-assistant/';
		console.log('mac assistant window - URL passed');
	}
	else
	{
		upassistWin.focus();
		console.log('focus on mac assistant window set');
	}

	return upassistWin;

	//window.open("/api/upgrade-assistant/", "macupassistant", "scrollbars=1,resizable=0,location=0,height=500,width=500,top=300,left=300");

}
